// GitHubActionStep represents the YAML lines for a single step in a GitHub Actions workflow
type GitHubActionStep []string

// Interface Segregation Architecture
//
// The agentic engine interfaces follow the Interface Segregation Principle (ISP) to avoid
// forcing implementations to depend on methods they don't use. The architecture uses interface
// composition to provide flexibility while maintaining backward compatibility.
//
// Core Principles:
// 1. Focused interfaces with single responsibilities
// 2. Composition over monolithic interfaces
// 3. Backward compatibility via composite interface
// 4. Optional capabilities via interface type assertions
//
// Interface Hierarchy:
//
//   Engine (core identity - required by all)
//   ├── GetID()
//   ├── GetDisplayName()
//   ├── GetDescription()
//   └── IsExperimental()
//
//   CapabilityProvider (feature detection - optional)
//   ├── SupportsToolsAllowlist()
//   ├── SupportsMaxTurns()
//   ├── SupportsWebFetch()
//   └── SupportsWebSearch()
//
//   WorkflowExecutor (compilation - required)
//   ├── GetDeclaredOutputFiles()
//   ├── GetInstallationSteps()
//   └── GetExecutionSteps()
//
//   MCPConfigProvider (MCP servers - optional)
//   └── RenderMCPConfig()
//
//   LogParser (log analysis - optional)
//   ├── ParseLogMetrics()
//   ├── GetLogParserScriptId()
//   └── GetLogFileForParsing()
//
//   SecurityProvider (security features - optional)
//   ├── GetDefaultDetectionModel()
//   └── GetRequiredSecretNames()
//
//   CodingAgentEngine (composite - backward compatibility)
//   └── Composes all above interfaces
//
// Usage Patterns:
//
// 1. For code that only needs identity information:
//    func processEngine(e Engine) { ... }
//
// 2. For code that needs capability checks:
//    func checkCapabilities(cp CapabilityProvider) { ... }
//
// 3. For backward compatibility (existing code):
//    func compile(engine CodingAgentEngine) { ... }
//
// Implementation:
//
// All engines embed BaseEngine which provides default implementations for all methods.
// Engines can override specific methods to provide custom behavior.
//
// Example:
//   type MyEngine struct {

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cat > /tmp/repro_engine_version.go <<'GOEOF'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"strings"

	"github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/workflow"
)

func main() {
	expr := "${{ inputs.engine-version }}"
	failures := 0
	check := func(name string, steps []workflow.GitHubActionStep) {
		joinedParts := []string{}
		for _, step := range steps {
			joinedParts = append(joinedParts, strings.Join(step, "\n"))
		}
		joined := strings.Join(joinedParts, "\n---\n")
		if strings.Contains(joined, "run: npm install -g @example/pkg@"+expr) || strings.Contains(joined, "run: ${RUNNER_TEMP}/gh-aw/actions/install_copilot_cli.sh "+expr) {
			fmt.Printf("%s: unsafe raw expression interpolation found\n%s\n", name, joined)
			failures++
		}
		if !strings.Contains(joined, "ENGINE_VERSION: "+expr) || !(strings.Contains(joined, "@$ENGINE_VERSION") || strings.Contains(joined, "install_copilot_cli.sh $ENGINE_VERSION")) {
			fmt.Printf("%s: missing safe ENGINE_VERSION env usage\n%s\n", name, joined)
			failures++
		}
	}
	check("npm", workflow.GenerateNpmInstallSteps("@example/pkg", expr, "Install Example", "example", false))
	check("copilot", workflow.GenerateCopilotInstallerSteps(expr, "Install Copilot"))
	if failures > 0 {
		panic(fmt.Sprintf("%d failure(s)", failures))
	}
}
GOEOF
go run /tmp/repro_engine_version.go
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_engine_version.sh

--engine filter to gh aw logs command\",\"body\":\"This PR adds the ability to filter workflow logs by agentic engine type using a new `--engine` flag for the `gh aw logs` command.\\n\\n## What's Changed\\n\\nThe `gh aw logs` command now supports filtering logs by agentic engine type (claude, codex):\\n\\n```bash\\n# Filter logs to show only Claude engine runs\\ngh aw logs --engine claude\\n\\n# Filter logs to show only Codex engine runs  \\ngh aw logs --engine codex\\n\\n# Works with other filters too\\ngh aw logs weekly-research --engine claude -c 10\\n```\\n\\n## Implementation Details\\n\\n- **New Flag**: Added `--engine` flag with validation for \\\"claude\\\" and \\\"codex\\\" values\\n- **Engine Detection**: Uses existing `extractEngineFromAwInfo` function to read engine information from downloaded artifacts\\n- **Filtering Logic**: Filters runs after artifact download by checking the engine type in `aw_info.json` files\\n- **Backward Compatible**: All existing functionality remains unchanged when no engine filter is specified\\n- **Comprehensive Testing**: Added tests for flag validation and engine filtering functionality\\n\\nThe filtering works by downloading workflow artifacts and examining the `aw_info.json` metadata to determine each run's engine type. Runs that don't match the specified engine filter are skipped (with verbose logging), and the command continues fetching more runs until the requested count of matching runs is found.\\n\\nFixes // isGitHubActionsExpressionString reports whether value is a single GitHub Actions
// expression (for example, "${{ inputs.engine-version }}"). Such values are
// evaluated by GitHub Actions before the shell starts and must be passed to shell
// commands through environment variables, never interpolated directly into run:.
func isGitHubActionsExpressionString(value string) bool {
	trimmed := strings.TrimSpace(value)
	return strings.HasPrefix(trimmed, "${{") && strings.HasSuffix(trimmed, "}}")
}

	// directly into run:, because the evaluated expression text would become shell
	// syntax. Put expression versions in an env var and expand that variable in the
	// shell command instead.
	globalFlag := ""
	if isGlobal {
		globalFlag = "-g "
	}
	installCmd := fmt.Sprintf("npm install %s%s@%s", globalFlag, packageName, version)

package workflow

import (
	"fmt"
	"strings"

	"github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/constants"
	"github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/logger"
)

var nodejsLog = logger.New("workflow:nodejs")

// GenerateNodeJsSetupStep creates a GitHub Actions step for setting up Node.js
// Returns a step that installs Node.js using the default version from constants.DefaultNodeVersion
// Caching is disabled by default to prevent cache poisoning vulnerabilities in release workflows
func GenerateNodeJsSetupStep() GitHubActionStep {
	return GitHubActionStep{
		"      - name: Setup Node.js",
		"        uses: " + GetActionPin("actions/setup-node"),
		"        with:",
		fmt.Sprintf("          node-version: '%s'", constants.DefaultNodeVersion),
		"          package-manager-cache: false",
	}
}

// GenerateNpmInstallSteps creates GitHub Actions steps for installing an npm package globally
// Parameters:
//   - packageName: The npm package name (e.g., "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
//   - version: The package version to install
//   - stepName: The name to display for the install step (e.g., "Install Claude Code CLI")
//   - cacheKeyPrefix: The prefix for the cache key (unused, kept for API compatibility)
//   - includeNodeSetup: If true, includes Node.js setup step before npm install
//
// Returns steps for installing the npm package (optionally with Node.js setup)
func GenerateNpmInstallSteps(packageName, version, stepName, cacheKeyPrefix string, includeNodeSetup bool) []GitHubActionStep {
	return GenerateNpmInstallStepsWithScope(packageName, version, stepName, cacheKeyPrefix, includeNodeSetup, true)
}

// GenerateNpmInstallStepsWithScope generates npm installation steps with control over global vs local installation
func GenerateNpmInstallStepsWithScope(packageName, version, stepName, cacheKeyPrefix string, includeNodeSetup bool, isGlobal bool) []GitHubActionStep {
	nodejsLog.Printf("Generating npm install steps: package=%s, version=%s, includeNodeSetup=%v, isGlobal=%v", packageName, version, includeNodeSetup, isGlobal)

	var steps []GitHubActionStep

	// Add Node.js setup if requested
	if includeNodeSetup {
		nodejsLog.Print("Including Node.js setup step")
		steps = append(steps, GenerateNodeJsSetupStep())
	}

	// Add npm install step. GitHub Actions expressions must not be interpolated
	// directly into run:, because the evaluated expression text would become shell
	// syntax. Put expression versions in an env var and expand that variable in the
	// shell command instead.
	globalFlag := ""
	if isGlobal {
		globalFlag = "-g "
	}
	installCmd := fmt.Sprintf("npm install %s%s@%s", globalFlag, packageName, version)
	installStep := GitHubActionStep{
		"      - name: " + stepName,
	}
	if isGitHubActionsExpressionString(version) {
		installCmd = fmt.Sprintf("npm install %s%s@$%s", globalFlag, packageName, engineVersionEnvVar)
		installStep = append(installStep,
			"        env:",
			fmt.Sprintf("          %s: %s", engineVersionEnvVar, strings.TrimSpace(version)),
		)
	}
	installStep = append(installStep, "        run: "+installCmd)
	steps = append(steps, installStep)

	return steps
}
package workflow

import (
	"fmt"
	"strings"

	"github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/constants"
	"github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/logger"
)

var copilotInstallerLog = logger.New("workflow:copilot_installer")

// GenerateCopilotInstallerSteps creates GitHub Actions steps to install the Copilot CLI using the official installer.
func GenerateCopilotInstallerSteps(version, stepName string) []GitHubActionStep {
	// If no version is specified, use the default version from constants.
	// "latest" means the installer will use the latest available release.
	if version == "" {
		version = string(constants.DefaultCopilotVersion)
		copilotInstallerLog.Printf("No version specified, using default: %s", version)
	}

	copilotInstallerLog.Printf("Generating Copilot installer steps using install_copilot_cli.sh: version=%s", version)

	// Use the install_copilot_cli.sh script from actions/setup/sh
	// This script includes retry logic for robustness against transient network failures.
	// The script downloads the Copilot CLI using curl with hardcoded github.com URLs
	// and does not use gh CLI, so GH_HOST does not affect the download. No step-level
	// GH_HOST override is needed here; the correct host is already set in GITHUB_ENV
	// by configure_gh_for_ghe.sh (or by the Derive GH_HOST step when DIFC proxy is active).
	stepLines := []string{
		"      - name: " + stepName,
	}
	if isGitHubActionsExpressionString(version) {
		stepLines = append(stepLines,
			"        env:",
			fmt.Sprintf("          %s: %s", engineVersionEnvVar, strings.TrimSpace(version)),
			fmt.Sprintf("        run: ${RUNNER_TEMP}/gh-aw/actions/install_copilot_cli.sh $%s", engineVersionEnvVar),
		)
	} else {
		stepLines = append(stepLines, "        run: ${RUNNER_TEMP}/gh-aw/actions/install_copilot_cli.sh "+version)
	}

	return []GitHubActionStep{GitHubActionStep(stepLines)}
}
package workflow

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"strconv"
	"strings"

	"github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/logger"
	"github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/stringutil"
)

var engineLog = logger.New("workflow:engine")

const engineVersionEnvVar = "ENGINE_VERSION"

// isGitHubActionsExpressionString reports whether value is a single GitHub Actions
// expression (for example, "${{ inputs.engine-version }}"). Such values are
// evaluated by GitHub Actions before the shell starts and must be passed to shell
// commands through environment variables, never interpolated directly into run:.
func isGitHubActionsExpressionString(value string) bool {
	trimmed := strings.TrimSpace(value)
	return strings.HasPrefix(trimmed, "${{") && strings.HasSuffix(trimmed, "}}")
}

// EngineConfig represents the parsed engine configuration
type EngineConfig struct {
	ID               string
	Version          string
	Model            string
	MaxTurns         string
	MaxContinuations int    // Maximum number of continuations for autopilot mode (copilot engine only; > 1 enables --autopilot)
	Concurrency      string // Agent job-level concurrency configuration (YAML format)
	UserAgent        string
	Command          string // Custom executable path (when set, skip installation steps)
	Env              map[string]string
	Config           string
	Args             []string
	Agent            string // Agent identifier for copilot --agent flag (copilot engine only)
	APITarget        string // Custom API endpoint hostname (e.g., "api.acme.ghe.com" or "api.enterprise.githubcopilot.com")

	// Inline definition fields (populated when engine.runtime is specified in frontmatter)
	IsInlineDefinition bool   // true when the engine is defined inline via engine.runtime + optional engine.provider
	InlineProviderID   string // engine.provider.id  (e.g. "openai", "anthropic")
	// Deprecated: Use InlineProviderAuth instead. Kept for backwards compatibility when only
		copilotInstallLog.Print("Skipping AWF binary installation (custom command specified)")
		// Return empty step - custom command will be used in execution
		return GitHubActionStep([]string{})
	}

	// Use default version for logging when not specified
	if version == "" {
		version = string(constants.DefaultFirewallVersion)
	}

	stepLines := []string{
		"      - name: Install AWF binary",
	}
	if isGitHubActionsExpressionString(version) {
		stepLines = append(stepLines,
			"        env:",
			"          AWF_VERSION: "+strings.TrimSpace(version),
			"        run: bash ${RUNNER_TEMP}/gh-aw/actions/install_awf_binary.sh $AWF_VERSION",
		)
	} else {
		stepLines = append(stepLines, "        run: bash ${RUNNER_TEMP}/gh-aw/actions/install_awf_binary.sh "+version)
	}

	return GitHubActionStep(stepLines)
}

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cat > /tmp/repro_engine_version.go <<'GOEOF'
package main

import (
    "fmt"
    "strings"

    "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/workflow"
)

func join(steps []workflow.GitHubActionStep) string {
    parts := make([]string, 0, len(steps))
    for _, step := range steps {
        parts = append(parts, strings.Join(step, "\n"))
    }
    return strings.Join(parts, "\n")
}

func mustSafe(name, out, raw string) {
    if strings.Contains(out, raw) {
        panic(fmt.Sprintf("%s has raw expression in run command:\n%s", name, out))
    }
    if !strings.Contains(out, "ENGINE_VERSION: ${{ inputs.engine-version }}") {
        panic(fmt.Sprintf("%s missing ENGINE_VERSION env:\n%s", name, out))
    }
    if !strings.Contains(out, `"$ENGINE_VERSION"`) {
        panic(fmt.Sprintf("%s missing quoted ENGINE_VERSION shell expansion:\n%s", name, out))
    }
}

func main() {
    expr := "${{ inputs.engine-version }}"
    npm := join(workflow.GenerateNpmInstallSteps("@example/pkg", expr, "Install Example", "example", false))
    copilot := join(workflow.GenerateCopilotInstallerSteps(expr, "Install Copilot"))
    mustSafe("npm", npm, "run: npm install -g @example/pkg@"+expr)
    mustSafe("copilot", copilot, "run: ${RUNNER_TEMP}/gh-aw/actions/install_copilot_cli.sh "+expr)
    literal := join(workflow.GenerateNpmInstallSteps("@example/pkg", "1.2.3", "Install Example", "example", false))
    if !strings.Contains(literal, "run: npm install -g @example/pkg@1.2.3") || strings.Contains(literal, "ENGINE_VERSION") {
        panic("literal version behavior changed:\n" + literal)
    }
    fmt.Println("ok")
}
GOEOF
go run /tmp/repro_engine_version.go
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_engine_version_runtime.sh

package main

import (
    "fmt"
    "strings"

    "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/workflow"
)

func join(steps []workflow.GitHubActionStep) string {
    parts := make([]string, 0, len(steps))
    for _, step := range steps {
        parts = append(parts, strings.Join(step, "\n"))
    }
    return strings.Join(parts, "\n")
}

func mustSafe(name, out, raw string) {
    if strings.Contains(out, raw) {
        panic(fmt.Sprintf("%s has raw expression in run command:\n%s", name, out))
    }
    if !strings.Contains(out, "ENGINE_VERSION: ${{ inputs.engine-version }}") {
        panic(fmt.Sprintf("%s missing ENGINE_VERSION env:\n%s", name, out))
    }
    if !strings.Contains(out, `"$ENGINE_VERSION"`) {
        panic(fmt.Sprintf("%s missing quoted ENGINE_VERSION shell expansion:\n%s", name, out))
    }
}

func main() {
    expr := "${{ inputs.engine-version }}"
    npm := join(workflow.GenerateNpmInstallSteps("@example/pkg", expr, "Install Example", "example", false))
    copilot := join(workflow.GenerateCopilotInstallerSteps(expr, "Install Copilot"))

        panic("literal version behavior changed:\n" + literal)
    }
    fmt.Println("ok")
}

+// isGitHubActionsExpressionString reports whether value is a single GitHub Actions
+// expression (for example, "${{ inputs.engine-version }}"). Such values are
+// evaluated by GitHub Actions before the shell starts and must be passed to shell
+// commands through environment variables, never interpolated directly into run:.
+func isGitHubActionsExpressionString(value string) bool {
+	trimmed := strings.TrimSpace(value)
+	return strings.HasPrefix(trimmed, "${{") && strings.HasSuffix(trimmed, "}}")

@@ -11,21 +12,33 @@ import (
 
 var engineLog = logger.New("workflow:engine")
 
+const engineVersionEnvVar = "ENGINE_VERSION"
+
+// isGitHubActionsExpressionString reports whether value is a single GitHub Actions
+// expression (for example, "${{ inputs.engine-version }}"). Such values are
+// evaluated by GitHub Actions before the shell starts and must be passed to shell
+// commands through environment variables, never interpolated directly into run:.
